        window.__LOCALE__ = "pt";

        function getLocationOrigin() {
            var origin = window.location.origin;
            if (!window.location.origin) {
                origin = "//" + window.location.hostname + (window.location.port ? ":" + window.location.port : "");
            }
            return origin;
        }

        function isMobile() {
            return navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Mobile') !== -1 || navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Android') !== -1;
        }

        function reportBI(extension, src, evtid, report) {
            var path = getLocationOrigin().indexOf("wix.com") > -1 ? "//frog.wix.com/" : "//frog.wixpress.com/";
            var date = new Date().getTime();
            var finaleReport = "";
            if (typeof report !== "undefined") {
                finaleReport = report + "&";
            }

            if (extension === "hp") {
                finaleReport += "origin=" +window.location.host+ window.location.pathname + "&";
            }

            finaleReport += "_=" + date;
            var imgSrc = path + extension + "?src=" + src + "&evid=" + evtid + "&version=adi homepage&" + finaleReport;
            var img = new Image();
            img.src = imgSrc;
        }

        reportBI('hp', '19', '315');

        function clearVideos() {
            var video = document.getElementById('video-player') === null ? false : document.getElementById('video-player');
            if (video) {
                video.parentNode.removeChild(video);
            }
        }
        var clearVideosSrc = setTimeout(clearVideos, 7000);
        function canPlay() {
            if (!new RegExp(['MSIE', 'Trident', 'Edge'].join('|')).test(navigator.userAgent)) {
                clearTimeout(clearVideosSrc);
                var video = document.getElementById('video-player') === null ? false : document.getElementById('video-player');
                if (video) {
                    document.querySelector('.video-player-bg').style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        video.play();
                    }, 400)
                }
            }else {
                var video = document.getElementById('video-player') === null ? false : document.getElementById('video-player');
                if (video) {
                    video.style.display = 'none';
                    var home = document.getElementById('home-fold');
                    home.style.backgroundImage = 'url(//static.parastorage.com/services/wix-homepage-davinci/1.216.0//images/header.jpg)';
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

   function getLocationOrigin() {
        var origin = window.location.origin;
        if (!window.location.origin) {
            origin = "//" + window.location.hostname + (window.location.port ? ":" + window.location.port : "");
        }
        return origin;
    }

    var pageOrigin = getLocationOrigin();

    function frogEvent(e)
    {
        e.preventDefault();
        var button = e.currentTarget;
        var frogType = button.getAttribute("frog-type");
        if (frogType)
        {
            var dest = button.getAttribute("href");
            var name = button.getAttribute("frog-name");
            var target = button.getAttribute("target");
            new Image().src = "//frog.wix.com/hp?src=19&evid=312&type=" + frogType + "&url=" + dest + "&button_name=" + name + "&origin=" + dest;
            window.open(dest, target);
        }

    }
    var frogs = document.getElementsByClassName('frog');
    for (var i = 0; i < frogs.length; i++)
    {
        frogs[i].addEventListener('click',frogEvent,true);
    }
</script>
